# Reference 4 for websocket-patterns


## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.

## Detailed Architectural Overview
+---------------------------------------------------+
|                  SYSTEM CORE                      |
|                                                   |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  | Component A +-------> Component B       |      |
|  |             |       |                   |      |
|  +-------------+       +-------------------+      |
|                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------+

## Algorithms and Formulations
The expected latency is calculated as:
L_total = L_network + L_processing + L_queue
Where:
L_queue = \lambda / (\mu (\mu - \lambda))

## Code Examples
```python
def process_data(data):
    # Process the data with complex algorithm
    return [d * 2 for d in data if d > 0]
```

```typescript
interface Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[];
}
class DataProcessor implements Processor {
    process(data: number[]): number[] {
        return data.filter(d => d > 0).map(d => d * 2);
    }
}
```

## Best Practices and Anti-Patterns
- **Best Practice**: Always validate inputs at the boundaries.
- **Anti-Pattern**: Using global state for concurrency management.
